he noho makemake hokotahi no
ina kui riva
he too mai i te kaha vai he ui aroto a te kaha vai
he oo te kohu o makemake kiroto ki te vai
he ui makemake ko toona kohu ariga ku oo a kiroto ki te vai
he ki makemake he aroha ki toona kohu
aue ropa e
ka maitaki koe ki a au
he papakina mai te manu ki te hoto matau o makemake
he veveri makemake he ui mee gutu mee kara mee huruhuru
he too mai e makemake he hakapiri he hakarere
he poki atariki te kohu o makemake
he noho he manau makemake mo aga i te tagata mo tuu peia mo rere mai o te reo mo vanavanaga
he tuki makemake kiroto ki te maea
ina kai rivariva ihoiho ki komea mee rakerake
he tuki hakaou kiroto ki te vai
i ava i paroparoko
he tuki hakaou makemake ki roto ki te oone rapo
he poreko mai te tagata
he ui makemake ku rivariva a
he ui hakaou makemake kai riva i horeko
he hakahauru i te tagata iroto i te hare
ki hauru he oho atu te atua amakemake he tuki kiroto ki te ka vakava o te kaokao maui
he poreko mai te vie
he ki amakemake
vivina vivina hakapiro e ahu e
ko makemake te tagata he rae
he too mai makemake i te kaha vai he hakapu he tuki
i ava i parokoroko
ina kai rivariva te aga
he too hakoou mai makemake i te maea he hakapu he tuki
ina kai riva takoa
ihoiho ki komea
he hoki hakaou makemake he puke i te oone he hakapu he tuki
he tagata mo noho i te kaiga
o te kope aure auviri ko porotu i vanaga mai
te kaiga o rapanui kaiga nuinui i te nohoga tuai a
pe he kaiga ana o hiva te nuinui takoa
o te tagata ko uoke i ketu i hakaemu i te kaiga
te ua i itiiti ai te kaiga o rapanui
hai oka i ketu ai i te kaiga e uoke
he ketu he oho mai mai hiva a he tuu mai ki pukopuhipuhi
he ketu ira he hati te oka a uoke
he toe mai o te kaiga nei ko te pito o te henua
penei i vanaga mai ai aporotu
he tagata tonei i tuu mai ai a kua ira a kua raparega
gata vake te igoa
kai agiagi e kua raparega te hakaaraga o gata vake
ko hogi atua kava aure auviri i vanaga mai
kaiga nuinui te kaiga nei
te ua i itiiti ai te kaiga nei ko uoke i ketu hai akauve i emu ai i te kaiga
o te tagata kikino o te pito o te he nua oira i ketu ai uoke ka itiiti ro te kaiga nei
mai te pito o te henua i ketu i oho mai ai ka tuu ro ki te tomona o gata vake ka tuu ro ki te ohiro
he tomo a te rotomea he iri he noho i vai marama
i te rua o te marama i iri ai ki te vare
i ka ui atu ko uoke e ketu e oho no mai a ki te henua he ki agata vake ki a te ohiro
he emu te kaiga ko taua te ika
ku ki ro ai a te ohiro
ki tata venavena atu he tata venavena he tata venavena
ko pukopuhipohi i hatu ai te akauve a uoke ka toe inei te tomoga o gata vake
te kaiga o hotu matua o hiva te igoa maori igoa nuinui
te kona noho o te ariki hotu matua i hiva marae rega
te matua o hotu matua ko taane arai
ko hotu matua te poki i hakaariki
te vie a hotu matua vakai aheva
te taina tamahahine o hotu matua ava reipua
te kona noho o te ariki tamahahine oava reipua i hiva marae tohia
he ui te ariki ku garo a te kaiga ki te vai kava
tai ua he garo
he pae te mahigo he mamate te tagata te vie te poki te korohua
he oho mai te tagata ko hau maka ariki
he moe i te po hau maka he hauru he oho mai te kuhane he tomo a te motu te kuhane o hau maka
he ui hau maka ko te motu
he ki te kuhane o hau maka he nape te igoa o te motu
ko ga kope tutuu vai a te taaga a hau maka i hiva
he oho mai te kuhane o hau maka he tomo kiuta ki te karikari he ui ko te pu mahore ahau maka he oho te kuhane o hau maka kiruga he tikea te rano
he nape i te igoa o te rano
ko te poko uri a hau maka i hiva
he oho te kuhane a te aro era e rarama a i te maara mo tomo kiuta ohotu matua
he oho a te ara he tikea te kohe
he rei hai vae he hati te kohe he ki te kuhane o hau maka
ko te hatiga o te kohe a hau maka i hiva
he oho he tuu ki poike he vari ki te aro nei
he oho mai a te aro nei he tuu ki taharoa
he ki te kuhane o hau maka
i ana nei te maara o te ariki
he oho mai he tuu ki haga hoonu
he tikea te one omua o te haga he ki hakaou
i ana nei te maara o te ariki ko hotu matua
he oho mai he tuu ki ovahe he tikea te one one uraura he vari mai ki anakena he tikea te one he ki hau maka
i ana nei te maara nuinui te haga nuinui mo tomo o te ariki ohotu matua
he garo ki hiva he veveri he ara he a he koa
he ui mai te tagata te igoa ko ira ki a hau maka
pehe koe e a ena
he ki hau maka
e ara no ana okoe
he ki mai aira
e ara no ana au
he ui mai aira
he aha koe e a ena
he ki hau maka
he kaiga iroto i te raa iruga
ka oho korua ka ui i te kaiga mo noho o te ariki ohotu matua
he oho mai ehitu gaio
te tagata rae te igoa ko ira te rua tagata ko raparega te toru tagata kuukuu ahuatava te ha tagata ko rigirigi ahuatava te rima tagata ko nonoma ahuatava te ono tagata uure ahuatava te hitu tagata ko makoi rigirigi ahuatava
hokohitu ga poki ariki ariki paka
he oho mai mai hiva iruga i te vaka
he ki hau maka
ana oho korua ana tomo korua kiuta e ui atu korua ki te motu ko ga kope tutuu vai a te taaga
he oho mai he tomo ki haga tepau he hakarere i te vaka i haga tepau
he iri mai he ui i te rano ina kai tikea he tikea te pokopoko itiiti he ki
ko te poko uri o hau maka
he reoreo ina kai tikea te rano
i tomo mai era kiuta he noho he keukeu i te uhi he oka akuukuu i oka te uhi
he oho ananake a te aro era he tikea te kohe he ki
i ana nei ko te kohe ku hati a i te vae o te kuhane o hau maka
he oho he tuu ki poike
he oho mai he vari ki te aro nei he ui i te one o taharoa one itiiti
he oho mai he tuu ki haga hoonu he ui one itiiti
he ki aira
ina he kona nei mo tomo o te ariki
haga itiiti ina eko rivariva ana tomo te ariki
he maruaki
he rere kihaho ki te tai ananate te tagata
he ea mai te ika kiuta hai hakari no he i te ika kiuta
he nape i te igoa
ko te kete kauhaga
he ui aira araparega ina he ahi mo tao o te umu
he hakauga mai erua gagata erima e noho ki te ahi iruga i te vaka
he oho mai kiruga ki te vaka he too i te ahi he hoki mai he mau mai i te ahi ki haga hoonu
he too mai i te ika he papa iruga i te maea
he too mai i te hukahuka makoi he tutu i te ahi he tunu he ootu
he kakai ahihitu
he makona he nape i te igoa o tou ahi era
ko te ahi tunu makoi a ira a raparega
he ui atu ahihitu tagata ko te honu ku tomo mai a kiuta ki te haga
he kuhane tae he honu
he kuhane i tute takoa mai ai
he kakata he oho mai a te ara ahihitu
i ui era te honu ku oho mai ana te hihitu he oho takoa te honu ahaho a te tai
he tuu aira araparega ki ovahe he tuu ananake he tikea te one one itiiti
he vari mai ki te paiga nei ki anakena he tikea te one nuinui
he koa he kakata he ki
i ana te maara o te ariki ohotu matua mo tomo kiuta
he turu ananake
ku tomo a te honu ki hiro moko
he oho te kope rae ko ira he ketu mai te honu kai gaei
he oho karua kai gaei
he oho katoru kai gaei
he oho kaha kai gaei he oho karima kai gaei he oho kaono kai gaei
he ki akuukuu
i a au te honu era he gaei mai
he ki a ira a raparega
ka oho ka ketu mai
he oho kuuhuu he ketu mai he gaei he amo he iri
ku garoa a te honu te ki akuukuu i aia ana gaei mai
i avaava era te honu kiruga he hapaki hai kapeu
he mate he mamae he haguhagu
he oho atu tou tika era he kakata o kuukuu te papaku ku mamae a i te honu he tupa mai te papaku kiroto ki te karava he hakamoe
he tere te honu he hoki ki hiva
he ki mai te reo o kuukuu
e ui korua e ga hoa e e ui korua o hoa ro i aau
he ki ananake
ina matou eko hoa i akoe
he reoreo
he too mai i te maea he hakatuu i te pipihoreko katahi pipihoreko karua pipihoreko katoru kaha karima eono pipihoreko maea
he ki ananake aono ki te maea
ana ui mai akuukuu
he korua e ga hoa e
ka ragi korua
i matou
he ki te maea
ku mao a
he hoa i akuukuu he tetere mai he oho mai a te ara he tuu ki hagaroa
he ui akuukuu
he korua
he ragi atu te pipihoreko
i matou
he koa kuukuu
he ui hakaou mai he ragi hakaou atu
i matou
he mate kuukuu
ku oho mai ana aira araparega hokoono he oho mai ki hagaroa kimua ki te haga he noho he ui ki te garu iruga i te papa ihaho i te tai
he vanaga ira ararua ko raparega he oho mai te vave
he ki
ko ruhi ki te rara matau ko pu ki te rara maui
etahi tuitui reipa i te gao o te moai ko hinariru
etahi i te pei eko ravaa evaru kaukau i te pei a i garo ro ai i hiva i te kaiga
e hakarogo atu a ko makoi rigirigi
mai hagaroa i iri ai ki orogo
i tuu atu ena ku tupu a te poporo o te uhi a ira
he tuu he vere kai oti
he ki aira
kaiga kino
he aga i te hare he keukeu i te hare mo moe
he popo kiroto ki te hare he ahiahi he hauru
he ki ko makoi ki arigirigi
e ara mai koe ki uimai au ki aira ki araparega ki toou o te honui
kokoe mo noho mai iruga i te kaiga nei ko matou mo hoki ki hiva ki te kaiga
e ui tou hauru anira i te po
he momoe
he ao ao nui
he ui ko makoi ki aira ki araparega
pehe korua e vanaga era
he ki raparega
mo aha aau e hagupotu e
he ki
ka vanaga mai ki maau
he ki aira
ka ui tou eete era ana hauru
ku hauru a
he gatu hai vae
ka tagi tou gogoro ki hakarogo mai aira
he gogoro reoreo
he vanaga mai ira

he garoa e tou kope hauru reoreo era he koa mo hakamaa ki te mahigo ko ga kope mo noho mai nei iruga i te kaiga nei
erima mo hoki ki hiva iruga i te vaka
he popohaga
he ki aira araparega
ka oho ka oga te miro o te ariki ohotu matua
he oho he oga he ui ki motu nui
ko te miro e hakapipiri ro a ararua
he ragi mai
i te miro a o te ariki
he oho aira araparega he oga he ui mai orogo ko te miro
he ragi

he ki te ariki
ka hakahoki
kaiga kino hoki kahukahu oheke tai ua ka okooko tai pa paku ka ora
he ragi
kaiga kino hoki kahukahu o heke tai ua ka okooko tai papaku ka ora
he ki aira
ki a tatou a tatou ka ragi tahaga no
he ragi ira
miro tamaaroa mo oho a hotu iti miro tamahahine mo oho anei
o hotu matua te miro e oho ara o ava reipua anei
he ragi ira
ahaho a te miro ana oho te ika kino te ihu roroa o tama
he oho
he hakamanamana te ariki tamaaroa hotu matua i te hakanonoga
he oho mai te miro a te aro era a te aro nei
he oga mai te miro o hotu matua ki variga te toremo
he ui mai te ariki ku tuu atu ana te miro o ava reipua ariki tamahahine ki motu kau
he rutu mai hotu matua
ka hakamau te konekone
he oho mai ki taharoa he poreko te haahaa roroa
he oho mai ki haga hoonu he poreko te kovare he oo mai ki anakena he papakina te ranu
el tapon mocoso entraron en anakena y salio el liquido amniotico
he poreko te poki a te ariki ava reipua
he ragi hotu matua he ui
tamaaha te ariki ena
he ragi mai te tagata
tamahahine

tamaaroa

ka hakauga mai

apo

matu ki oho ki te kaiga rivariva

ku nuinui a te poki atariki ko tuu maheke
he maruaki te poki he tagi ki te matua tamahahine ki te kai
he oho mai hotu matua he ui e tagi a te poki
he ragi hotu matua
ki te aha ro koe e tagi ena
tae koe he ariki ka mou te morore rakerake puoko havahava
he tagi te poki he hakama o te ragi i toona morore
he ki te poki iroto i te inaga
he momore ro au e ragi mai era ahotu matua
poki ke o au tae o au aana poki ke o te tahi tagata
he tagi nuinui
he hoki te ariki ahotu matua ki toona hare
he tagi te poki
he tuu mai te matua tamahahine he ka i te umu mo tao o te uhi o te ku mara
he taomi i te kumara mo kai rae o te poki
he ootu he uru i te umu he tao i te umu
he mau i te kumara taomi he vaai ki te poki
ina kai kai
he ui te matua tamahahine ko vakai ki taana poki ku ahuahu a te mata i te tagi haga ku rari a te ariga i te matavai he ki
he aha koe e tagi ena
he ki te poki
he ragi mai o tou tagata rakerake ena
he ki te matua tamahahine
pehe i ragi mai ai ki a koe
he ki te poki
penei i ragi mai ai
ka mou te morore rakerake puoko havahava
he riri te matua tamahahine he ki
a koro ana koe tae koe he morore
he oho mai te ariki ahotu matua ki te kai ku maruaki ana
te ariki tamahahine ina kai vaai i te kai ku riri a vakai mo hotu matua o te ragi i te vanaga rakerake ki te poki
he ki ahotu matua ki vakai mo avai i te kai he pae te taua
he ki vakai ki a hotu matua
o te aha koe i rago ai ki tou ate i te vanaga rakerake
he ki hotu matua
ina au kai ragi he poriko taa kope ena
he ragi vakai
tae he morore te poki nei aau mau te poki nei
kokoe a te morore rakerake puoko havahava a tai amahiro
ko kohiri tuu hogohogo te hagai i tua i otioge o hiva
he ragi hotu matua o te aha koe i tae haaki mai ai mai noho ana i hiva i te kaiga oira au ka oho mai mai hiva ki te kaiga nei
ana koe i ki mai ki aau he morore au ina au eko oho mai mai tooku kaiga
he tagi te ariki hotu matua he tere ki hare moa viviri
i iri noho ai ko hotu matua he noho hokotahi
he aga i te aga he hua te uhi te kumara te toa
he oho atu avakai ki hare moa viviri
he tere hakaou te ariki ahotu matua ki hare moa tataka
he hua te kai
he oho atu vakai ki hare moa tataka
he tere te ariki ki te gao o te honu ararua ko taana maaga hagai tamaaroa itiiti
he oho hakaou atu te ariki tamahahine vakai ki te gao o te honu
he tere ahotu matua ki taro tataka he oho hakaou atu te ariki tamahahine
he tere ahotu matua ki akahaga
he oho atu te ariki tamahahine
he mamae te ariki vakai he mate
he muraki iruga i te ahu te igoa o te ahu ahu aturehoa
he noho te ariki tamaaroa ko hotu matua i akahaga ananake te mahigo e aga i te vai
te poki rae a hotu matua ko tuu maheke te rua poki ko miru te matanui te toru poki ko tuu te matanui te ha poki ko hotu iti te mataiti
ku korohua a te ariki he iri ki te rano he noho i te rano
te igoa o te hare ko te vare te reigataki
he too mai i te maea hahati he hono i te maea hahati he ki te ariki
ko te maea hono a hotu matua
aga mauga
he mamae te ariki
he oho mai te mahigo ka rau ka rau ka piere ka piere
he ki te ariki ki taana ga poki
ka oho mai korua ananake he mate au
he oho mai te ga poki he tuu ki a hotu matua he aroha
he ki te ariki
koai koe
he ki te poki atariki
koau nei ko tuu maheke
he ki te ariki
ina koe eko ravaa e te atariki e
one nui i anakena i toou kaiga koura nui i toou kaiga
he ea te poki atariki kihaho he uru te rua poki ko miru te matanui he aroha
he ki te ariki
ina koe eko ravaa mo roou o toou mahigo
he ea kihaho te rua poki
he uru te tora poki ko tuu te matanui he aroha
he ki te ariki
koai koe
he ki
koau nei ko tuu te matanui a hotu matua
he ki mai te ariki
ina koe eko ravaa kikiri nui i haga tepau pipi nui i te hue
he ea te poki
he uru te hagupotu ko hotu iti te mataiti he aroha
he ui mai te ariki
koai koe
he ki atu
koau ko hotu iti te mataiti a hotu matua
he teki he hogi i te kukumu ararua paiga
he agiagi e te ariki poki rivariva poki hiohio
he ki te ariki
ina koe eko ravaa e hotu iti e e te mataiti a hotu matua e
he niuhi tapakai i motu toremo hiva i tou kaiga
he ki te ariki
ka nonoho mai korua taaku ga poki i tooku puoko i tooku vae i te kaokao
he nonoho
he ki te ariki ki taana maaga hagai maaga tamaaroa
ka oho koe ki huareva ki te vai mouga maaku mo unu
ana unu au i te vai era he mate au
he oho he too i te vai he uutu i te vai he mau he oho kiroto ki te hare he hakarere i te vai
he ki te ariki ohotu matua
ka hakaunu mai
i hakaunu era he horo i te vai kiroto ki te manava
he ki hakaou te ariki
ka hakarogo mai tokorua tariga ki taaku vanaga mouga
he ragi au ki hiva ki te kaiga ki te ariki
he ki te ga poki ki te mahigo ananake
he ragi te ariki ki hiva
e kuihi e kuaha
ka hakaooa itiiti mai koe i te reo o te moa o ariage
he ooa mai te moa mai hiva ka tuu ro mai te reo o te moa ki te kaiga neicanto el gallo desde el continente llegando su voz hasta esta isla
ooa take heuheuooa take heuheu
he mate te arikimurio el rey
vanaga mouga o te ariki ohotu matuaestas eran las ultimas palabras del rey hotu matua
he too mai te ga poki i te rago he hakaeke i te papaku he tupa i te papaku
he oho he tuu ki akahaga
he keri i te rua ka hoa ro kiraro nui
he paega hai keho he hakatopa i te papaku i a hotu matua kiraro ki te rua
he oho mai te poki atariki ki te puoko etoru ga poki o hotu matua i te vae
he tanu hai oone ko te oone ko te mee rakerake kakai
he puoko ina kai tanu hai mee rakerake
hai one i tanu ai
o te poki atariki i tanu ai hai one
he haga ko te poki atariki mo hore o te puoko mo toke
he oti te tanu
he po
he tiaki e raua e te ga poki
he ki te poki atariki ki te poki rae
ka oho koe ka hauru
he oho te poki rae he hauru
he ki hakaou ki te rua poki
ka oho koe ka hauru
he oho he hauru
he ki ki te toru poki
ka oho koe ka hauru
he oho he hauru
he noho te poki atariki hokotahi no
he popohaga he mataki he hore mai i te puoko he tanu hakaou i te rua
he ea te poki atariki he too mai i te puoko he tere he mau i te puoko he naa
he tuu ki te tahi raa he ui ko te takaure ku muia a te takaure
he mau ki te tahi kona te raa he hoki he ui ku muia a te takaure
he mau ki te tahi kona
he piro
he hakahopu i te puoko he tata he mau mai ki patuga
he kakaro i te maea maea oraro
he kakaro ite maea oruga mo pua
he viri hai kahu i te puoko he hahao kiroto ki te maea he pua aruga hai rua maea he hakarere i te puoko o te ariki ohotu matua imua i te hare ka moe no te puoko
he oho te poki atariki ki hiva
ku korohua a
ku garo a ina kai agiagi hakaou e te poki atariki
he oka te maika o te tagata etahi ko ure honu ataka te igoa
i vai poko te hare noho oure honu
i te rua o te marama he oho ure honu he rapu i te maika he vere
i te raa rae he horihori he hakarere i te oka
he tere te kioe he tute kai ravaa
ka porua raa he tute hakaou kai ravaa
ka potoru raa kai ravaa
ka poha raa kai ravaa
ka porima raa kai ravaa
ka poono raa he kero te maika he hakamao te kahui mouga
he tikea hakaou te kioe he tere
he tute
ku kava a te manava
he oo kiroto ki te maea
he kikio mai te reo o te kioe
he okaoka hai miro
he vouvou mai
he kuhane o hotu matua tae he kioe
he ketu i te maea he hahata
he tikea te puoko e hai ro a hai nua
he too mai he mataki
ko te puoko hakahuru hai pua
ai te nuinui o te puoko kotetu ka maitaki te puoko
he mau he oho kiroto ki te hare he tau iroto i te hare hoou
ina kai agiagi e ure honu te puoko penei puoko ariki ina
he tere te kahi aure honu he here te koreha he puhi te ura he puhi te umu he tao i te kumara he uga mai te rogo aure honu ki te ariki ki a tuu ko iho ki te hare kai
he oho tuu ko iho koia ko toona mahigo te vie te poki te tagata te korohua he tuu he kai te gogoro o te hare hoou o ure honu
he uru te ariki kiroto ki te hare hoou etahi uka tamahahine iroto i te hare mo hokorua o te ariki ana kai
he kai te ariki ararua
he oti te kai he moe te ariki kiraro hakaora
he ui te mata aruga he tikea te puoko
he tagi tuu ko iho ku maa a i te puoko puoko ariki o hotu matua
he ki tuu ko iho
ka moe mai te niho kai honu kai kepukepu o hiva o te kaiga
he garoa te tagiga o tuu ko iho e te uka tamahahine hokorua era
he iri te rima o tuu ko iho he too mai i te puoko he hahao kiroto ki te kete he ea mai roto mai te hare he tere mai he tuu kiroto ki toona hare hare hakahaere i te moai i tore tahuna
he keri i te rua i te haha o te hare he paega i te rua he too mai i te puoko he hakatopa kiraro ki te rua
he pua aruga hai keho he tanu hai kirikiri he tanu hai oone he reirei hai vae ka kikiu ro
he noho te ariki
i te rua o te marama he ui ure honu ina he puoko oroto o te hare ku too a
he a a he auau he ui ki te uka tamahahine hokorua era o tuu ko iho
he to tau puoko
he ki te uka

he ki ure honu
pehe i ki ai
e tagi a ki te puoko
ka moe mai te niho kai honu kai kepukepu o hiva o tomatou kaiga
he kava te manava o ure honu mo tuu ko iho o te toke mai i taana puoko he agiagi iho e ure honu puoko ariki ohotu matua
he uga te rogo ki te tagata he oho mai mai anakena
i oho mai te tagata karau karau kapiere kapiere
he oho mai he tuu ki ki tore tahuna kimua ki te hare o te ariki ko tuu ko iho te tagata a ure honu

he ki te ariki
kai agiagi mai

ki mouga
ko arone rapu i vanaga mai ai
te maori aga hare a hotu matua ko nuku kehu toona igoa
i a ia te hare te aga

i oti era te ato i hu era te tokerau he marere te hare kiraro

te ua e marere era te hare i te tokerau te tau te tau

he hakarere e te hanau momoko he ki te hanau momoko
ka hakarere atu te hoou mo hakarahi o toona o te mahigo
he hakarere
i po era he ea mai roto mai te vai te hanau eepe he tere ki mauga toatoa he tuu ki te hare o te hanau momoko te igoa ko pipihoreko
lira i noho ai aororoine
he moe ki te vie hanau momoko he tupu te poki tamaaroa oroto o te vie hanau momoko o te ure o haoa
he rahi te mahigo ka kauatu ka kauatu ka rau ka rau
he oho mai te tahi mahigo hanau eepe ki tahai
i iri noho ai
he tomo mai te miro o kape he tikea e te kape i te hanau eepe he vaai i te kaha ava i te kai ki te hanau eepe
ina kai kai ina kai unu i te ava
i too no mai he hopu he huri ki te puoko i te ava
te moai i aga ai e te hanau momoko
te moai rae ko tai ahare atua
ina kai rivariva
o te maori omiru i aga te moai ina kai ravaa
he ki ki te tagata hokoono
ka oho korua aono ki te veravera ki te hare o kave heke o marama marama o tuu
ka ki ki a kave heke koia te maori
pehe te agaga o te moai
he oho mai aono gaio he tuu ki te hare o kave heke
he ui mai kave heke ko te repa riva hokoono
i a te repa riva
he aroha te repa riva
e korohua he koe
he ki mai kave heke
i au kohomai korua ko ga kope
he ea kave heke he ka i te umu
he ahiahi he maoa he hakauru
ai ka too ka kai mo hatu o mahaki
he ki tou gaio era eono
ku agiagi a
he momoe i te po he ui kave heke
ai ai ai pehe korua ko ga kope i oho mai ena
he uga mai matou e te hoou e miru ahotu ki a koe
he ui akave heke
ki te aha
ki te agaga o te moai
pehe te agahaga o te moai
ina he reo kai rere o kave heke
he moe i te po ka potahi raa ka porua raa ko te potoru raa i aroha ai
he ki kave heke
ka noho anira
he ka i te umu he maoa i te popohaga he hagao he aroha
he ea mai tou gagata eono mai roto mai te hare kihaho he oho a te ara he tuu ki te aro o te maea kihikihi
he ea akave heke ki te tara o te hare he ragi mai
e kau a repa e
ka noho ka hakarogo mai ki te vanaga ka ragi atu ena au e hakarogo rivariva mai
he kiki aono
ka noho tatou ki ragi mai te hoou akave heke
he nonoho he ragi mai kave heke
ka oho e ki ki te hoou ki a miru ahotu ki a tagi teako ahotu iraro i akorua ana te moai
he oho he hipa etahi kope he mimi
he ragi
na iraro i a korua ana ka ui ka ui ahara ka tae haaki mai te hoou akave heke
mee rakerake he kinoga oira i tae haaki mai ai
he oho he tuu ki te rano rarako
he ui mai te matatoa
pehe korua ga kope
he ki ki a miru
ka tata oho mai matou
i ragi mai ai te hoou akave heke
ka oho ka ki iraro i akorua ana te moai
he ki te tagata aga moai
ka pao te moai ka aga
he aga etahi moai tamaaroa etahi moai tamahahine
he rivariva te moai
he koa

he mau he hoa kihaho ki te tai

he mau kiruga ki te hu papaku mo tiaki o te avaga o te ahu papaku mo ira i aga ai
he ki
ana i mate akave heke ina eko agiagi mai te agaga o te moai maea
etahi nuahine ka umu mo te tagata aga moai
ka rau ka rau ka piere ka piere te tagata aga moai
ananake te raa e tahu era te nuahine ka unu mo te tagata aga moai
i tuu era ki te tahi raa kai tuu hia mai te nuahine ka umu
i maia ro ai i te umu e te tagata umu ura
he kai
he tuu mai te nuahine
he ui ku maoa a te umu kai toe te ura i kai tahi no e te tagata he pae
ina kai vaai i te kai mo te nuahine ka umu
he tagi te nuahihe he ragi ki te moai
ka papagahaa korua ko ga kope ka hihiga kiraro
he hihiga te moai
he turu tou tagata era etahi ka tapa ro ki tai
he too mai i te kupega he turu he rere kihaho ki tai
he ruku iroto i te pu ura he uru kiroto
he hakarogo te tagata era irito i te pu ku haro aruga
he huri he ui atu
i ka ui atu ena ko te ura iruga he ea mai kihaho
he oho atu he tomo kiuta he ki ki te gagata erua
koho mai tatou ki rere
he rere atotoru he tuu ki te kona pu era
he ruku atotoru
he ui atu ku turu mai a te ura mai ruga o te pu
he iri atu te rima atotoru he aaru he mau mai kihaho he hakakau kiuta ka tomo ro
he iri kimua ki te hare
he tao he kai
kotetu ko te ura rarape nui
he kai he oti
he topa mai te ruau ka umu mo te tagata aga moai he ki
a ura ke kotetu ko te ura rarape nui
hokohia korua i kai ai i a tetu i te ura rarape nui
kai toe korua etahi vae maaku
he hoki te ruau he ragi aruga a te ragi
ka hihiga korua ko ga kope
he hihiga te moai kiraro
he hu te tokerau te ui ra te patiri he heruru i te po
i te rua raa ku hihiga a te moai
he marere te pukuraga he oho
ko te tokaga te moai mauga
ina kai aga hakaou i te moai
te miro rae i tomo ai ki te pito o te kaiga ko voro te igoa
etahi tagata oruga o te miro ovoro i noho ai iruga i te kaiga i piko mai ai
te ua i piko mai ai o te ki o te tagata honui oruga o te miro mo tigai o te tagata iruga o te kaiga nei
ko moaha te igoa o te tagata i piko ai i mauga toatoa
i te po ha raa o te miro i piko ai
te po tahi raa he tau te taua te taua o te tagata oruga o te miro ki te tagata oruga o te kaiga nei
ka po rua raa o te taua ka po toru raa o te taua
i te po ha raa i te ahiahi i mamate ai te tagata erua i ooka no hai kakau
te igoa o te tagata i mate ko pau ko motunui tagata rapanui
no aga o te hare he hao i te maea paega he vari ki te pini
kioti te hao te paega he hou ite pu hai toki he akatuu i te oka oka piko he hakapiri te oka ki te hahaga he here hai hau hau kaka maika hau inahute
hare hahau etoru hahau eha hahau erima hahau eono e huru o te mahigo hare
he ki te ariki ohotu matua tuko iho ki toona tagata e hahau i te hare a te matau peira te pito poki te vaka te kupega mo te ika a te matau
ana tae rivariva te hahauhaga he mamate te tagata he higa te hare i te tokerau peira te vaka eko ravaa te ika anatae rivariva te hahauhaga
kioti te oka te hakatuu he eke te kaukau mivo
kioti te kaukau he pua te hatuga kiruga
he here i te kaukau mivo i te hatuga he here
kioti te rau toa he eke te mauku kiruga ki te rau ton he here
ina eko oo te ua
peira te agahaga o te hare o te mata amua
i te hare o te gagata o te mata mua ina he roi
te tagata ivavo a te moegahaga
he mauku te mee heriki ovoto o te hare
he moega te mee heriki ana moe i te po
he too mai etahi maea regorego pavavaha mogarua he hahao kiraro ki te moega

kioti te huhuti i te gaatu he too mai he mau ki te hare

ki pakapaka te gaatug he too mai he tui i te gaatu hai hau paka

etahi korohua i vanaga mai ki a au ananake hare etahi tagata hakarogo ki te taua ana tuu mai ki te hare tutu i te po
ina eko pua i te nua
hai mee nua itiiti ana pua ki te hoto ai ka vereri no i te po i te takeo
koai ite te taua te tuu mai ki te hare tutu i te po ki rivariva ai ana tere te tagata i te po
i te nohoga tuai era a te kahu uru o te gagata o te ga vie he nua mahute
no aga o te nua he pao mai i te mahute

he kiri mo too mai te kohau mo hoa
he mau i te kiri he turu ki tai he pua hai maea hehaka para iroto i te vai

ki pakapaka he too mai he tia mo te nua mo uru o te uka mo uru o te repa mo uru o te tagata hoki mo te kahu puo po
e iku te nua mo te uka huru hare mo te repa huru hare
te nua rakerake mo te ga mee haere tahaga no o te ara

kioti te titigi i te pua he too mai i te pahoa nua he hai i te pua kiroto ki te pahoa nua
kioti te hai he tatau kiroto ki te taheta
kioti te tatau kiroto ki te taheta he too mai i te nua he tuki tuki hakamotamota mo hakatau

he hakarere

he tia te nua he too mai i te paoa hare nua mo hore mo hakatitika i te nua

ata ku maa a i te tagata o te mata amua

ina he tagata uriuri

mai hagapoukura ki vaihu te kona noho o te ganatimo

te umu o te paega tamaaroa mo te paega tamahaine

pe too me e a te hakaara haga

ka too e te ariki e

ina he tagata mo tuu ki anakena kiruga ki te one
te tagata mo tuu ki anakena kiruga ki te one he ariki he ga poki o te ariki he tuura he vie o te ariki
ana oo te ga poki ke ki anakena kiruga ki te one he too mai he tigai

i ui atu era ika hiva ku oho mai a te tagata ki a ia
he tere ika hiva he tere he garo
he ragi e te ariki poki
ka hakarere ina eko tigai aaku a i ragi mo oho mai mo kokori omaua inei
he hakarere e te taua ina kai kimi i a ika hiva e haka rere atu
te mee he puke he oone i puke hai rima mo mimiro o te ga paki iruga i te pake
te poki mo mimiro iruga i te puke etahi te agahuru matoru tau te tamaaroa te tamahahine
he oho mai te matua he ui i taana poki iruga i te puke
he too mai te gagata i te mukomuko he verovero ki te poki tahuti ahaho a te puke
ana tuu te mukomuko mee tae rivariva eko ro a te tau ana mate ro o te pokituu mukomuko
te poki tae motu i te mukomuko e koa no toraua matua kai motu i te mukomuko
he hoki te ga poki te matua ananake ki te hare
he ka i te umu mo takapu o te poki o te raua mimiro haga
he makoi mo hakanini mo hakareka o te uka o te repa o toraua huruhaga iroto i te hare
he ako
ka nini te makoi nau opata karatuu te makoi
miro rakerake ka nini nini koe te makoi oone o te rano e kau era
he makoi mo hakareka takoa o te neru iroto i toraua ana
he ako
kahuru koe e neru e i te ana tautau ipu kiea
nai te nohoga tuai a te mee he garu ka tuu ro mai ki te nohoga nei
he rae ana hakagaru hai papa
he rere he hau he iri kihaho ki te tai
he kau he iri ka tuu ro ki te kona hakaeke garu
he tata mai te vave he tuu mai ki tua ki te kauha
ki eke mai te vave he hoa i te papa kinua he eke te uma kiruga ki te papa he moe mai kiruga
he hati he oho mai te vave he oho mai te garu he tomo ki a rio
garu mo tomo ki a rio garu mo tae tomo e hatipu no te vave
ki maa i te hakaeke hai papa he hakamaa i te haka honu
i vaega ana o te papa ana hakamaa ana hakahonu mai
ki maa te hakahonu ai ka iri ki te kona hakaeke garu mau ana haka honu mai
hakahonu mo tomo ki a rio hakahonu mo tae tomo e hatipu no te vave
te hakahonu i hakamaa ai mo te vaka emu
ku maa a i te hakahonu ina eko haga ki te papa
ana ai te papa ka hakagaru mai
ana kore te papa e hakahonu no mai mo tomo kiuta
he poreko te poki he hagai ehitu tau he nuinui he mau te matua i te poki ki tua ki te ana hueneru he hakarere
ananake te matua he mau i toraua ga poki etahi poki erna poki
ote ariki i ki mo mau i toraua ga poki ki tua ki poike ki te ana hue neru te poki tamaroa te poki tamahahine
ina eko kai i te kumara
te mee mo kai he toa paka he pipi he pure
e hue ro a iraro i te ana hueneru
ina he tagata eko tuu kiraro ki te kona ana
he matua tamaaroa no te mee mo tuu ki te ana hue neru mo mau i te kai
he nunui te naru tomaa roa te neru tamahahine i kumi te puoko o te neru i kuni takoa te akikuku
ina eko tope
ana ea mai te neru kiruga kiroto ki te tagata he mamate
ke mo mate ke mo ora
ana mate te neru he tagi te matua
ka huru koe neru e ka huru ka hakaritorito koa nerwe i te ana tautau ipu kiea o ga neru tuai koro hora kaea kiruga i te toga katopa kiraro ka huru ka ritorito neru e
te tupuna o tooku matua poreko keri muti te igoa i vanaga mai i te neru te neru tamaaroa neru tamahahine
he toa paka no te kai
te kona noho i tua i poike iroto i teana te ana te igoa ko te ana hue neru i more matpuku te ana nuinui
ananake te tau oraua te reka kaikai hakahiti iruga i te rima
i kuni te maikuku ikumi te rauoho ka topa ro ki te vae
i kahu pua te rauoho o te neru
ai ka noho no
i te nohoga tuai era a o te mata amua te poki mee hakarogo ki te vanaga o toona matua
ana riri te matua ina eko rere te reo
nahoga tapu o te poki i te matua
ana tae hakarogo te poki ki toona matua he too mai i taana poki he ki
ka moe kiraro
e hakarogo no te poki ki te vanaga o toona matua
he moe te poki kiraro
he too mai te matua i te oka he tutu ka matematero
kioti te riri o te matua he hakarere he ki ki taana poki
e ui koe o mahani hakaou te tae hakarogo mai ki a koro kia nua
ana tae hakarogo mai e tutu no au i a noe hai oka ka mate ro
ana tutu te matua y taama poki he hakarogo he rivariva
ana poki rakerake ki toona matua he tarotaro e te matua i taana poki mo mate
he too mai i te oone he kai he ki
nee kikino ho noe
ana kai i te oone eko hini he mate taane poki
hai moa hoki ana too mai he tanu ora i te moa kiraro ki te oone he puoko mo hakaoga
he rua mee nei ana too mai e te matua ana aga mo taana poki mo mate
ana haga hai oone
ana haga hai moa
i te nohoga tuai era a te poki ina eko kimi i te vie e ia a
mo te matua e kimi te vie mo te poki
i te rikiriki haga a ana oho te matua ana kimi mai hai poki tama hahine mo taana poki tamaaroa
he too mai te matua o te poki tamaaroa i te poki tamahahine kiroto ki toona hare he tahu i te umu mo toona hunoga
ki nuinui ai ka moe ki taana poki tamaaroa
ki moe taana poki tamaaroa ki te poki tamahahine he hatu te matua ki taana poki
ina eko tiagi te hunoga o uri te mata
e tigai poki no
ana tae haga te poki tamaaroa mo moe he tohi e te motua ki taana poki tamaaroa he tohu penei
mee kikino ho koe
he  tohu ki toona hunoga tamahahine
eko ravaa koe e hunoga e e tetea ro tou mahigo
e roou no te hugavai ki toona hunoga
ki tuu ki tahi marama he puhi te umu e toona hugavai
he tao te moa te uhi
he uga te rogo ki te matua o te uka
he oho mai te matua ki te umu kai o toona muko o te haka hoki haga i taana vovo
ki tuu mai toona matua he tari te kai kai hakahoki i taana vovo ki te rima o toona matua
kioti te umu te tari he tagi te hugavai mo toona hunoga
he tagi mai te hunoga mo toona hugavai
kioti te tagi he aroha ki toona hugavai
kioti te aroha he oho ararua ko toona matua ki te hare
ina he matua o te poki tamaaroa eko roou hakaou pehe nohoga era a e noho era ararua ko toona hunoga
te poki tamaaroa ina eko ravaa te tau ana mate ra
mee tohu o toona matua ina eko ora
te urumanu ina eko moe ki amiru e moe te urumanu ki te urumanu a
e moe te miru ki te miru a koia te poki mo ariki te poki omuri ina eko ariki
ki rivariva ai te hakaara haga o te mahigo e moe te niru ki te niru a
peira te urumanu ki rivariva ai te toto o te urumanu ana hakaara i toona mahigo
e ui te niru ki te vie mo moe
he aha koe
ana ki
he urumanu au
ina eko moe
ana ki mai
he niru au
ka moe ki rivariva ai toona mahigo te toto o niru
he tohu he uruga o te ariki tuai
tahataha o tai te puvai i tahai
te vai tehe mai uta i te tai papaku
ana tehe mai he ua mai te tai
he piri te vai kara ki tou vai magaro era
he noho eko tehe hakaou mai
ana kore vai ua he turu toatou ki tahai ki te vai uutu mai mo unu mo tunu mo te kai
ananake te raa he turu te puaka te hoi ki te vai unu i tahai
he oti a te kona vai o matou e too mai nei
ana kore te ua i te tuai haga era a te ariki paka he rako ki te ua mo hoa mai
he turu ki tai e te tagata rako ua he too mai i te maea karakala te igoa i te miritono takoa
he iri hokotahi no kiruga ki te mauga he hakarere i te maea iraro a i te mauga
he tuu kiruga he rako
e te uka matavai roa ahiro e
ka rei mai koe kiraro i te matava
he turu mai te tagata rako ua he oho he tuu ki vaega ki te kumaka ki te maika ki te uhi
he too mai i te maea i te miritono he hahao kiraro ki te oone
ki hahao i te maea i te miritono kiraro ki te oone he hoa te ua
he keri i te umu mo tao i te kai
he too mai i te hukahuka hepenapena he tutu he puapua i te maea kiruga ki te hukahuka ki ootu te umu
he too mai erna miro he uru te igoa he uru i te umu
ki herohero te maea he uru te umu
kioti te uru i te umu he haahei i te umu
he too mai i te mamoe he hoa kiraro ki te umu i te kumara takoa
he too mai i te maea he pua kiruga ki te kai
kioto te maea hepua te taueve kiruga ki te maea
kioto te pua te taueve he tanu hai oone
he noho he tiaki he hakahini hini ki ootu te kai
i te nohoga tuai era a umu keri okaoka umu pae te rua
te umu keri okaoka mo te tagata e ka te umu pae mo te vie e ka
he mee te ua o te umu kerioka oka ana tae ka e te vie o oone te vie i te tanuhaga i te umu keri akoako
umu pae te umu mo ka e te vie umu vie tae oone oira i avaai ai mo te vie e ka
te umu pae ana aga he keri te rua he too mai i te pae he hakatopa kiraro ki te rua eha pae erima pae
he komo hai maea rikiriki mo hakahiohio o te pae
kioti te komo he tanu hai oone a te tapa o te pae
kioti te tanu he ui ku rivariva a
ki ka te vie i te umu pae he toomai i te papa he hakatopa kiraro kite umu he too mai i te hukahuka he penapera etahi pu mo hakarere mo hakahahata a vaega ki rivariva ai ana tutu
he puapua i te maea kiruga ki te huka
kioti te puapua i te maea retoo mai i te rau toa he tutu
kioti te tutu he gatu kiraro ki te pu hehu te umu
ki hinihini te huhaga o te umu he ui te vie ku ootu a te umu
he too mai i te aovahu o te tahi umu he popko kiruga mo hakaootu rivariva o te maea o te umu
ki ootu te umu he too mai he uru hai uru i te umu
ina eko tanu hai oone e pua no hai taueve
he ki au ki osantiago
kuhaga a koe mo oho taua mo rama
he ki mai osantiago
ku mao a
he oho taua he rama
he too mai maua i te tuke he haka takataka he amoga he herehere kioti te herehere i te rama he oho maua ki tai he tutu i te rama hetikea i te ura
he aaru mai au i te ura hai rima he ragi atu au ki osantiago
ka mau mai i te kete mo hahao o te ura
eha erima ura i ravaa mai e maua
kioti te rama he vahi atu au i aia o te ura
he iri ro mai maua kiroto ki te hare
anira he turu ki tai ki te ura ruku
ki tuu ki tai he patu te kahu he too mai te hami
kioti te hami he too mai i te hio he tata hai vai
kioti te tata he too mai hepuru ki te mata
kioti te puru ki te mata he rere kihaho ki te vai he ara he ui araro o te vai ki tikea mai i te karava
he ruku he ui iraro i te karava ki te ura
ana ai te ura he too mai
ana kore ura he ara he ui i te tahi karava
te ura ana tikea he oho te rima he aaru mai a te vaero
he oho atu te rua rima he too mai a te ipu
ki ravaamai e te rima he iri mai he ea kiruga o te vai hemau he oho ki uta he hakarere iroto i te kete
kioti te hakarere he hoki hakaou he rukuruku
ki ravaa mai i te ura he hoki maiki te hare
he tuu mai ki te hare heka i te umu mo hoa mo tao i te ura mo inaki o te kumara
ki ootu te umu he maoa mai he apa kiroto ki te kete i te uru i te kumara he oho kiroto ki te hare hetoo mai i te ura he avavahi he kai
te mee rae mo aga he kupega
he pona i te kupega kiruga
ki te tutu
kioti te pona i te kupega he oho he too mai i te rimu he ruru
e ai ro a etahi pu mo ruru o te rimu
he too mai etahi kupega itiiti he pua kiruga ki te pu he vai toroto i te pu
he too mai i te rimu he haka eke kiruga ki te kupega he ruru
kioti te ruru he topa te koura kiraro ki te pu
he ao mai i te koura kiroto ki te kete he mau he haka rere iruga i te vaka
he too mai i te kupega he huki ki te kauha o te vaka
he tono i te vaka ki roto ki te vai
ki oo te vaka kiroto ki te vai he too mai i te maea he popo kiroto ki te vaka
kioti te maea te popo he eke te tagata kiruga ki te vaka hehoe he iri ki te hakakaga
he uimai a uta ki te pou o te hakakaiga he ui takoa ki te atua tapa
ki titika te vaka ki te pou he hoa hai maea
kioti te maea te hoa he hakamarere hai koura
kioti te hoa i te koura he too i te kupega he memere i te kupega he hakaturu ki vaega o te vai i te kupega iraro hehakanoho i te pupupa
etahi tagata mo mau mo hakanoho i te vaka hai mata kao etahi tagata maana e huti i te kupega
he oga te tagta huti kupaga araro he ui ki te tuu mai o te ature
ki tuu mai te ature kiruga ki te kupega he momotu i te kupega
he marere i te koura he paka mai te ature he kai i te koura
he ragi mai
ka mau mai i te vaka ka hakatitika
he haro mai i te kupega koroiti no he hakavaega i te ature kiroto ki te kupega
ki vaega te ature iroto i te kupega he haro mai he hakahorou
he pua hai hoe aruga a te vai mo hakaveveri o te ature
he moko te ature kiroto ki te kupega
he ui atu ku pura a te ature iroto i te kupega he irimai te kupega kiruga ki te vaka
he nanao mai i te ature kiroto ki te vaka
kioti te nanao mai i te ature he memere hakaou i te ku pega n mo hakaturu hakaou
hare hagu nuinui te tagata rivariva mo rukuruku iraro i te parera
hare hagu itiiti ina eko rukuruku i te kona parera
etahi raa he ea kihaho ki te tai etahi vaka
ko patea avaka ko rapahago ko kikorao te tahi hoki tagata he ara i te poa he turu ki tai he tuu he pona i te kupega mo te huti o te ature
kioti te kupega he hoho heruru i te rima
kioti te ruru i te rimu he tono i te vaka kihaho ki te tai he too mai i te maea he popo kiroto ki te vaka
he huki i te kupega i te kauha o te vaka
he eke te tagata kiruga ki te vaka he hoe i te vaka he iri kiruga kite hakakaiga
he ui ki te pou he hakatitika
he ui takoa ki te atua tapa
ki ui tu titika a te vaka ki te pou he hoa hai maea ki tikea e te ature ki oho mai
he nanao i te rimu mai roto i te kete he hoa kihaho ki te tai
he paka mai te ature he kai te koura
kioti te koura te hoa he too mai i te kupega he hahatu i te tau o te kupega he nanao mai i te rimu mai roto i te kete he pua kiruga ki te tau o te kupega he viri i te koura hai tau kupega he hakapune i te pupupa o te kupega o hiohio ki marere ai te koura
he hakaturu i te kupega he hakavaega he momotu mai i te kupega he marere te koura he paka mai te ature he  kai i te koura
he haro mai i te kupega hehakavaega koroiti o veveri te ature
he ui atu apatea ku oo a te ature ki vaega o te kupega
he haro mai he hakahorou
he pua hai hoe kiruga kite vai ki veveri teature ki moko kiroto ki te kupega
i oo era te ature kiroto ki te kupaga hemotu te pupupa o te kupega i te pagahaa o te ature
i motu era te kupega he turu araro
etahi tagata ko rapahago te igoa aana te kupega he too mai i te hau he nave hai hau i te hau
he ui mai patea
ina he reo o rapahago kai vanavanaga
he oti herutu patea ki te kupega he turu he oho he topa kiraro tu topa a te kupega ira e kiraro
he too mai i te tau o te kupega ki te rima he haro mai kiruga
ina kai gaei mai i te kupega
he too mai he hoa atu i te tau o te kupega he iri kiruga
i vaega mai era o te vai he hakarogo atu he pakakina mai te tapau ki te ariga
etahi tagata ko kikorao toona igoa aana i too mai i te tapau he here hai hau kiruga ki te tapau he hakaturu kiraro ki te parera
apatea he huri te ariga araro he turu he hoki koia ko tapau i te rima he tuu kiruga ki te kupaga he here hai hau i te kupega
he haro mai e ruga o te vaka
he ea kiruga he gaaha te toto a te tariga a te ihu hoki
he oho atu te vaka he hakapoa
he too mai e te tagata oruga o te vaka he aaru he hakanoho ki ora te hagu
itoo mai era kiroto ki te vaka he hoki mai ki uta kai iri kiruga ki te hakanonoga
he tomo ki uta
he iri mai patea ki toona hare hemoe mamae a
taganira he turu au ki tai hete i te koreha
he too mai erua miro
etahi miro mo hakapu he here te igoa
te rua miro ina eko hakapu he haka tatari te igoa
mo maunu o te ika kiruga mo hakatatari mai i te koreha kiroto ki te pu o te hau
he too mai i te hau he hakauru kiroto ki te pu o te here
kioti te hakauru he gita i te hau he hakateretere te hau ki rivariva ai ananita au i te koreha ka hiohio ro
he rae te maaga ana uruuru hai rima ki ravaa te maaga mo tigi tigi ai ka here i te koreha
ki ravaa i te koreha he too mai he avaava aruga a te maea he mate te koreha
kioti te avaava he too mai etahi maea mo tigitigi i te puoko o te koreha
he too mai he hahao kiroto ki te kete
i vavaa mai erima koreha
i te hora ahiahi au i tunu ai hai mori i paraipani ai
ki hinihini kuootu a
he too mai iraro he ao kiruga ki te mareti he kai
he rae ana moe te varua ai kaoho ki te kahi ki ravaa i te kahi
ana ui au ku ravaa a taaku oru i te po ku ravaa a te kahi
kutaia a au i te puaa ku ravaa a te kahi
ana motu ro te taura he motu te hau kahi
ana tae motu te taura ina eko motu te hau kahi
tooku hugavai ana oho ki te kahi hi e mau i te maea hitikakarega te igoa
ana mau i te maea ina eko kore te kahi
ana tae mau eko ravaa i te kahi
tooku tupuna etahi maea ko te takapau hakareva ateka te igoa iroto i te oone
ana haga ki te ika hahave he mataki mai i te maea he huri i te aro aruga
he oho mai te ika kiuta he hakapae
he hahave no te ika mo rere mai kiuta
ki i te ika iuta he huri hakaoa i te aro o tou maea era araro he tanu
he oti te ika inaeko rere hakaou mai
etahi raa he iri matou ko ko atepano ki hare oviki ki te humara hao
he ki mai atepano
ka oho katua mai te kioe mo tao iraro i te umu mo kai
he oho he tua mai erua te agahuru etoru te agahuru te kioe i ravaa mai
he too mai he rara he hakateetee i te kokoma he hoa te kokoma
kioti te hakateetee he hai hai rito maika he hai erima katahi poki
he tao
ki maoa he too mai he kai
katahi poki etahi aana hai karua poki etahi hoki aana hai
ana toe te toega he mau mai kiroto ki te hare mo te hora ki hauru
he kai he hakamao
i te nohoga tuai era a ina he puaa ina he mamoe o te pito o te henua
oira he huru o tomatou tupuna he kai i te kioe
ki ai te poki mamae he ka i te umu
i hakatano te roa o te poki mo tao iraro i te umu mo hakapaahia
iraro he maea vera iruga i te maea he toro maika iruga i te toro maika he mauku iruga i te mauku he moega
he poki he moe iraro i te umu kiruga ki te moega
hepua i te nua o hahau
he noho iroto i te umu he tehe te paahia
kioti te noho he ea mai te poki mamae he haere
ku oti a te mamae
ana tagata haoa toona gagata tuai era a he too mai i te kaha he huri i te vai kiroto he tunu i te maea ka vera ro he too mai he hahao kiroto ki te kaha mo hakaoera o te vai
ki vera te vai he hahao i te haoa kiroto ki te maahu
kioti he too mai he hakahopu he mau he hakamoe
he motu te haoa ina kai mate
he oho te matua o te haoa he haka uga ki te maori ko marioaoa
he ki mai ko marioaoa
ka hoki ka tunu te maea mo hakahopu o te haoa
he oho mai marioaoa hevere i te mahute o te haoa he ui he hakahopu mo too mai i te tuuria mata mai roto i te haoa
he tata ka maitaki ro he too mai i te ivi ivi o te gatu o te ivi heheu ivi reherehe mo rivariva ana kaui hai uaua o te kioe
he ki marioaoa ki te hoa ika
he mee o vaai hia ki te tahi maori
maaku ana e hoki mai e ui
ana ika pu more o te kopu ku momore ana te kokoma
e rivariva no i amarioaoa ana too mai i te kokoma mai roto mai te manava ana hakapiripiri te tahi potupotu o te kokoma ana kaui hai uaua o te kioe hai ivi o te gatu o te ivi heheu
eko rivariva te potu rikiriki o te kokoma ana kaui
ana potu rivariva no ka kaui hai uaua kioe
he hakahopu he rere i te haoa
etoru raa ana mataki hakaou
he too mai i te uhi he tao he ootu te umu he maoa
he too mai i te uhi etahi e marioaoa ana he hagai hai uhi ki te tagata haoa
he kai
he ui marioaoa
ka hakarogo ana topa ana oho ki tou kona kaui atu era e au
he ki mai te tagata haoa
ku topa rivariva ana tou uhi nei
he ki marioaoa
he riva koe
he oti he ea he hakaaroha marioaoa he hoki ki toona hare
i te toru o te raa ana mataki hakaou
koro riva ro eko hoki hakaou mai marioaoa
ka kau atu te maori ika o niru te maori rivariva ko marioaoa te igoa
ana moe te tagata papaku iroto i te hare he oho mai te ivi atua gavovo araaru varua
he ui i te mamae he tikea i te mamae oruga o te hakari
tae he mamae he hahati e te varua
he ki te ivi atua ki te poki ki te vie
tae he mamae te mee nei he akuaku
anira au ka haki mai i te ahiahi e too mai te kupega e pua kiruga ki te hare
ananake te kona ana viri haikupega ka hiohio ro ai korua kaea ro kihaho
ihaho korua ana noho ka hakarere no i te mamae iroto i te hare
e too mai korua i te hukahuka mo nio mo tunu i te akuaku ana ravaa e au
he hoki te ivi atua ki too na hare he noho he hakaahiahi
i te ahiahi ata he hoki mai he uru kiroto ki te hare te ivi atua
eko hini te nohoga he ui atu he tata mai te akuaku he uru mai te akuaku ki te mamae
he teki atu te ivi atua he aaru hiohio he neke te eve a te haha he ragi te reo ahao
e haho e ka tutu te ahi e hororou te ahi ka nio rakerake
ku hiohio ana e aaru era te ivi atua i toona rima
he hetu te ahi
he mau he hakauru kiroto ki te ahi

e ui era i te tagata i te hare koro i te paina i te hare hakama rogorogo i te hare hakama tau i te hare hakama kohau o te tagata mate i te hare hakama o te raga ki te hare kohau kiri tuku ki te atua kia rarai a hova
he ui mai era te mata o oroi ki te ariki kia hotu matua ka vari ro ahaha aro o te henua
he ui era hotu matua raua ko tuu ko ihu
he hiri oroi i te taura kumi mo te ika ko te ariki
he tuu ki tona ra he too a oroi he oho i te pu o te taura hiri era he haka pu i vaega o te ara he pua hai hatuoi mauku
he pu mai a hotu matua he ui oroi kia hotu matua
he ki oroi i roto ia ia ana
he mate koe ia au
he oho mai hotu matua
he tike ra e hotu matua tau me puapua era hai hatuoi mauku
ku maa ana te ariki a hotu matua he oho koroiti mai
he rei i te tapa o te taura a oroi i rei era
he ka riti e oroi i te taura ina kai hiohio te vae o hotu matua
he ki hoko tahino te ariki a hotu matua
he mate a koe ia au i tona raa
he oho hotu matua he tu ki ruahaua ki orohie
he ui ana i te tagata ki haga te tega he hoki mai
ku haka pu ana oroi i te taura mai roto mai toona hare ana i haka pu i oho ro mai ai te roaroa o te taura
he haka pu i te ara mo te ariki ko hotu matua
he pu hakahou mai o hotu matua
he tuu ki ruga ki tau taura era a oroi
he ui hotu matua i tau taura era
he oho te vae o hotu matua he eke he rei
he haro oroi he higa he haka higa hotu matua
he taliuti mai oroi he ea atu a hotu matua
he too mai ia oroi he tigai
he mate oroi he ariki oroi o hiva o marae rega

he hakaaroha mai kaiga ki a makita ki a rokeaua
he ragi kaiga
ka uru ki roto ki te hare
he uru makita rokeaua he noho
he momoe ararua ga io he hauru
he ka kaiga i te umu he tute mai i te moa he tigai he unu i te huhuru he rara he hakate i te kokoma he tata i te kokoma he hatui ki ruga ki te maea
he oho te maaga hagai a kaiga he mau i te kokoma ma makita ma rokeaua
he tuu ki roto ki te hare tau maaga hagai era
he vaai i te kokoma hatui ki a rokeaua
he ui mai rokeaua
he aha te mee na
he hakahoki te maaga hagai a kaiga
he kokoma moa
he ki mai rokeaua etahi tagata e hauru roa ana ko makita
he ki rokeaua
kaihaga maua mee tae kai kokoma moa maua mee kai kokoma tagata no maua
he to hakahou tau maaga hagai era a kaiga i tau hai kokoma moa era
he hoki he ki ki a kaiga
pe nei e ki mai era mee tae kai kokoma moa rauas
mee kai kokoma tagata no te e ki mai era ki a au
he ki kaiga
e ku mao a ka iri mahaki ka ragi ka iri mai
he iri tau maaga hagai era
he ea ki ruga he ragi
e maaga rakerake a kaiga e ka iri koe ka oho mai
he iri mai he piri he ki maaga rakerake a kaiga
ka po tahi raa i ragi hakariva ro mai
he tagi
ka moe mai te kaiga tutae teatea i te mahore aue te kaiga e ka moe mai raro te kaiga tutae teatea i te mahore

ka moe koe ki raro
he moe kaiga poki

he ara makita

matu ki iri

ku hakapu a i te nehenehera i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
ku hakapu a i te verira i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
ku hakapu a i te rekara i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
ku hakapu a i te maitakira i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
ku hakapu a i te rivara i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
ku hakapu a i te rivarivara i te ara ai ka hakanehunehu ro i te pu o te taura hai kiri hau o tikea e hotu matua ki oo te vae kiroto
